Homeless people and drug addicts frequent this park regularly so stay safe and never go to this park. This was my experience: I finally decided to try take my dogs to the leash free zone of Centennial park on Stockdale & Monclaire street. As soon as I got to the gate two elderly Animal Control Officers (one bald man and one woman) rapidly drove right up to the entrance and started asking me questions about my dogs and whether or not they are licensed. I was about to eat a hot lunch with someone else and wanted to eat in peace. After I provided proof my dogs are legal they continued talking to my friend and I knew the food was getting cold so I interrupted them and told them to move on. The man got extremely upset and walked over to the bench where I was sitting and got about 2 feet from where I was sitting and started aggressively staring down in my face and accusing me of being all sorts of names such as mentally ill, with "serious problems" etc. I felt extremely uncomfortable by this strange old man berating me at the park while my food was getting colder and colder and I stood up and asked him why he is harassing me and to just leave me alone because I proved I have the right to take my dogs to the park. He then got even more aggressive and hostile and threatened to call the cops and take me to JAIL! I told him he was the hostile one and I should be the one calling the police and the woman officer (whom appeared to be his partner/spouse) started grabbing him and trying to coerce him away from me and back in the car (which was an unmarked car and likely illegal BTW). He reluctantly obeyed her partners demands and left. While I was at the park I saw three dangerous looking homeless people (one of them was wondering around near the entrance of the dog park gate talking to himself) and 3 people doing drugs  30 yards from the entrance of the dog park gate. I felt disrespected, harassed, berated and unsafe and it was a HORRIBLE experience, especially when the authorities are focused on me and my legally licensed dogs while ignoring the real problems that were going on at the park right in front of them. Stay safe, be smart and AVOID THIS PARK.</review>

< Review>
They have some really good deals here. At this location the staff isn't overly friendly (one time they charged me for 1 item twice but I didn't realize it until I was leaving the parking lot, and since it wasn't expensive- & the receipt machine was conveniently not working, I let it go), but overall they are competent enough. They sometimes have fundraisers where they sell candy bars in a competition with other stores in the chain. I was happy when they put a Family Dollar out here, since it was a store I liked going to every so often. They dont have many shopping carts at this spot and you can't take it out of the store, which makes buying a lot of stuff... difficult.
You can get a soft throw for $5, name brand and generic medicine, makeup, towels, automotive  products, home decor (curtains, including black out curtains, rugs, wall decorations like paintings or word art, candles, frames, shower curtains, Glade plug-ins, etc.) and cleaning products (from sponges and dish soap to Swiffer products; brooms; window, toilet, & counter spray bottles; floor cleaners & bleach), gardening supplies (flower pots, soil, seeds), clothing (underwear, shirts, pants, pajamas, bathing suits & footwear) for women, men, and children, holiday decorations, candy, energy drinks and soda, arts and crafts supplies (coloring books, crayons, markers, highlighters, pens/pencils, etc.), greeting cards, cigarettes, some really nice curtains and bath mats, and and I'll surely for items that are discounted- their "red tag" sale items. <user_id>107914103284453188820<//user_id>< username>
Ryan Vallieu<//username>
<time>1563810288406< /time><Rate>5<//Rate>< text>
The online quote system doesn't seem to garner response, but definitely give them a PHONE CALL and they will set you up.  I searched online on their parts lookup system to verify they would have the part I was looking for, a rear passenger window to a 2012 Suzuki SX4.  SX4 are hard to source parts like this for since Suzuki left the US market in 2013.  Aftermarket support through the usual supply channels for the glass shops has dried up.

Cypress was very courteous on the phone.  They verified the part was in stock and pulled it and prepped it for pickup without requiring a down payment or payment.  They called like they said they would to let me know the actual part was ready for pickup.  They DO deliver to shops within 40 miles, but the shop we're working with to do the window replacement work told my wife (its her car) that they would not accept deliveries.  This is weird to Cypress and myself, but ok - they are local so we went to get the window ourselves.

The shop staff was friendly and was aware of our part being pulled.  The shop dog is the friendliest lab that has spot between the counters, and he loves pets! :D

This was a pleasant experience, and the window was inexpensive compared to other sources like Ebay with Chinese aftermarket glass available.  The window is in GREAT shape.  Sure it was dusty from being stored in a warehouse, but it cleaned up easily.

This is much better than having to crawl around a U-pull on your own with your tools trying to extract the proper parts, or even locating the desired vehicle, etc.  I'll gladly do business with them again.</text>

<userid>103687470950214091898<//userid>< text>
My husband and I and our pup lived here, all of 13 days. We moved in mid-June 18 and moved out by the end of the month!

We wanted to live in a cheaper area so we made the move from Sunnyvale to Milpitas. The rent was at a great (for the bay area) price point and the community was beautiful.
The community is still relatively new and had a modern/ upscale feel. We chose the 701 sq ft one bedroom with a beautiful pool view. The common areas and pool were well maintained. I loved the little conference areas and the pet walk!

We had a temp leaser at the time who didn’t really know the community but when Yolonda Longmire came back, from lunch, she was very friendly and helpful. She made the application and move-in process quick and easy!

The apartment was a little tight but we managed to fit and organize everything nicely. We had moved in and unpacked in 2 days (I hate clutter). I noticed a small bug in the kitchen cabinet while unpacking but assumed it was due to the apartment being vacant, killed it and continued unpacking. Immediately I noticed stains on the carpet and the bathroom and kitchen floor were dirty. When we walked barefoot our feet turned black. I informed Yolonda and this was easily remedied by the maintenance team. They came and re-cleaned and all was well or so we thought. On night three the nightmare began!

We had moved into an apartment that was infested with roaches! I say infested because that “harmless bug” I saw on night one was a baby roach!! Which was confirmed when the countless other baby roaches and full-on adult roaches started coming out of every nook and cranny! We immediately began to self treat and put in a Service Request for Pest Control. These pests were everywhere! I was afraid to cook to shower to sleep! They would run across the kitchen walls as I go to turn the light on. I found them in my clothing, in the closet and under our bed. We immediately talked to management because we knew we did not have roaches at our previous apartment. The actual manager was out on maternity leave so we were assisted by a temp, Kristy Howell, who was absolutely amazing!

Long story short, they scheduled Pest Control to come “check” our apartment. Because I also work in Property Management and know how these infestations work/ spread quickly, I requested that the surrounding units be checked as well. Come to find out the unit below me were LIVING WITH ROACHES and had not requested Pest Control which is why they came upstairs to our apartment so quickly! After further investigation, it was discovered that the first floor unit had put in a request to have that apartment treated for roaches. It was treated and they moved out but the roaches had made their way upstairs to the second floor. But they never requested treatment and we just so happened to move in on top of them!!

Kristy and Yolonda worked diligently to schedule treatment of our unit but I was completely freaked out and uncomfortable living there. Not to mention that Pest Control had to come to our home once a week... for the next three weeks to treat. So we would have to move our belongings to the center of our apartment every week! This did not make for bearable living conditions, as it was managements job to make sure the apartment was free of Pests when we moved in! So we threw away everything we owned for fear of bringing these pests to a new apartment. We spent $5000 to buy new furniture and $3000 on new clothing and necessities!!!

We broke our lease, without penalty, thanks to Kristy’s amazing efforts and moved out just as quickly as we moved in! So renters beware and check check check for bugs before unpacking!!< /text>

I have been living here for over 2 years now, I have seen managements change multiple times, some were good, others were not.
The current management is exceptional.

Pros:
-	Relatively newer community. Apartments are well constructed with Plenty of closets. Walls are thick, so your neighbors will not bother you unless they are unreasonably loud. All appliances, including in-home laundry, are relatively new and in good working condition.
-	Fitness Center, Swimming pool and common areas are maintained extremely well.
-	Close to public transport. The light rail and great mall transit center and literally within watchable distance.
-	Walkable distance to Great Mall and Century Theatres.
-	Smoke-free policy. This certainly helps to provide slightly cleaner air and also good for the kids.
-	Management that cares – based on my experience, this is one of the fewer communities where management takes active steps to resolve resident issues. There have been several issues with packages being stolen after being delivered at the front door. Management installed special electronic lockers and all packages are now delivered safely into the lockers. This is a much better option than waiting for the leasing office business hours to pick up packages or losing packages from the front door.

Cons:
-	Parking: Parking used to be easily available in the past but because of some recent changes, a free parking spot is not available later in the night. A parking permit does not guarantee a parking spot anymore. Assigned parking spots come at a price starting $100/month.<//Review>

<Review>I currently live in Ilara and have waited to write a review until now so I could really get a feel for the place.

Move in: The staff here are very nice, both office and maintenance staff, we had to wait awhile with some minor repairs when we moved into our unit that weren't fixed when we moved in but they were resolved without too much issue, we had our sink blow out in week 2 and our screen in our living room needed to be replaced, not too big of a deal the maintenance staff are great. We did get charged $100 for a late fee on our first months rent which was fine because we were a day late, the only problem with that was we never were really told how to pay our rent I guess you are just expected to figure it out online, oh and if you pay online you get hit with HUGE charges from the payment company, no joke, it's nuts.

Apartment: We really like the apartment honestly it's very modern and comfortable, there's lots of plugs for electronics and modern cable wiring for high speed internet which is a huge plus for young people. the bathroom is big in our unit but our bedroom is small, I honestly wish the bathroom was smaller and the bedroom bigger all of our bedroom furniture barely fits so you can walk around. Otherwise everything is great, we really like the place.

Security/Parking Garage: Here is the big issue with the complex that needs to be said, THE PARKING GARAGE GATE IS ALWAYS BROKEN! which means random people can bypass the whole stupid security system and go into the building and just walk around or vandalize peoples vehicles!!! Literally I've seen the gate wide open for strangers probably 30% of the time I've been here and it's honestly alarming, there is only passkey security on the first floor which makes sense....if the gate works or if people don't let strangers follow them through the gate. My girlfriend and I have had 4 packages stolen off our porch in the past week alone and there is 0 security once you get past the first floor. We are supposed to be getting parcel lockers at some point but as it stands we have lost $300 in products due to lack of security in the building and luckily our cars have been okay at least. This is the real reason for my poor review and the low rating does not go towards the staff here at all, literally the security needs to be increased here because it's just poor right now as it stands. There also seems so be a perpetual problem with people littering in the stairwells and parking garages which is totally a problem with the people living here and not an issue with the building or the staff here, the people here are just too lazy to throw their trash in the chutes or in trash cans.

I would absolutely bump this rating up if the package issue was solved, hopefully the new lockers fix this problem but the delivery drivers don’t always follow the instructions you setup for delivery.

***Updated Review***

On my updated review I can only give Ilara a 4 star review. We are talking about moving out soon to get away from the commercialized buildings because this one has basic security and is a target for theft. I have no way of knowing if it’s our neighbors taking things off our porch or if it’s someone getting into the building. Great family park. There is a water pad, playground, baseball diamond and exercise area. There are covered picnic tables. They have a rec center with sports sign ups. This is a great place to sign up if your little ones aren't yet into big organized sports or are just trying their hand at a new sport. The Easter egg hunt is fun.
